    { 1   ;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table50650;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                                RFE.COPY("Request for Exception");
                                RFE.FILTERGROUP := 2;
                                RFE.SETRANGE("No.","Request for Exception"."No.");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CompanyInformation.GET;
                                  CompanyInformation.CALCFIELDS(Picture);

                                   "Request for Exception".CALCFIELDS("Description of Request");
                                   IF "Request for Exception"."Description of Request".HASVALUE THEN BEGIN
                                    "Request for Exception"."Description of Request".CREATEINSTREAM(InStr);
                                    InStr.READ(DescriptionOfRequestTxt);
                                   END;
                                  //
                                   "Request for Exception".CALCFIELDS(Justification);
                                   IF "Request for Exception".Justification.HASVALUE THEN BEGIN
                                    "Request for Exception".Justification.CREATEINSTREAM(InStr);
                                    InStr.READ(JustificationTxt);
                                   END;

                                   "Request for Exception".CALCFIELDS(Remarks);
                                   IF "Request for Exception".Remarks.HASVALUE THEN BEGIN
                                    "Request for Exception".Remarks.CREATEINSTREAM(InStr);
                                    InStr.READ(RemarksTxt);
                                   END;

                                   IF STRLEN(DELCHR(DescriptionOfRequestTxt, '<>')) = 0 THEN
                                    DescriptionOfRequestTxt := NoRec;

                                   IF STRLEN(DELCHR(JustificationTxt, '<>')) = 0 THEN
                                    JustificationTxt := NoRec;

                                   IF STRLEN(DELCHR(RemarksTxt, '<>')) = 0 THEN
                                    RemarksTxt := NoRec;

                                   IF Cust.GET("Request for Exception"."Customer Dependecy") THEN
                                    CustomerDependecy := Cust.Name + ' ' + Cust."Name 2";

                                   IF Employee.GET("Request for Exception"."Documentation Engineer") THEN
                                    DocumentEngineer := Employee.FullName;

                                   IF Employee.GET("Request for Exception"."Person In Charge No.") THEN
                                    PersonIncharge := Employee.FullName;
                                END;
                                 }

                               "Record Link".SETRANGE("Record ID", "Request for Exception".RECORDID)

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  "Record Link".CALCFIELDS(Note);
                                  IF "Record Link".Note.HASVALUE THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(NoteText);
                                    "Record Link".Note.CREATEINSTREAM(Stream);
                                    BinaryReader := BinaryReader.BinaryReader(Stream,Encoding.UTF8,FALSE);
                                    NoteText := BinaryReader.ReadString;
                                    END;
                                END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
